{"nick":"joepie91","message":"christo_m: anyhow, summarizing the CommonJS-style model that I've worked out for Riot so far... a packageable component is a module that contains a .tag file and an index.js - the index.js first requires dependency tags, then requires its own .tag file (which should ensure correct loading order). it would depend on a bundler like webpack/browserify to resolve this. there's always a project-specific top-level <app>, but beyond that all communication","date":"2016-03-17T13:58:29.715Z","type":"message"}
{"nick":"joepie91","message":"between tags consists of events being emitted by child tags and methods being called *on* child tags. that way, none of the components needs to have any knowledge of either its siblings or its parent, only its children.","date":"2016-03-17T13:58:31.241Z","type":"message"}
